1773	TALLAHASSEE , Fla. 1996-12-06	B-LOC O B-LOC O
1774	Fourteen years after he bludgeoned and shot a man whose trailer home he robbed in 1982 , John Mills Jr .	O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O B-PER I-PER O O
1775	, 41 , was put to death in Florida 's electric chair Friday .	O O O O O O O O B-LOC O O O O O
1776	As Glenn Lawhon , a rural Florida minister who is the victim 's father , looked on , Mills was pronounced dead at 7:13 a.m. EST ( 1213 GMT ) for the murder of Lester Lawhon .	O B-PER I-PER O O O B-LOC O O O O O O O O O O O B-PER O O O O O O O O O B-MISC O O O O O B-PER I-PER O
1777	Speaking in Arabic , Mills made a final statement before an anonymous citizen flipped the switch that sent 2000 volts of electricity through his body , said Department of Corrections spokesman Eugene Morris , who was present at the execution .	O O B-MISC O B-PER O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O B-ORG I-ORG I-ORG O B-PER I-PER O O O O O O O O

1779	Prison officials said they had no record of Mills ' official conversion , but they said that , on May 14 , 1991 , he had asked that a new name , Yuhanna Abdullah Muhammed , be added to his prison file , which is usually an indication of a conversion to Islam .	O O O O O O O O B-PER O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O B-PER I-PER I-PER O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O B-MISC O

1782	He spent Thursday with family members and his spiritual adviser , Morris said .	O O O O O O O O O O O B-PER O O
1783	Mills was scheduled to die Wednesday but had his sentence temporarily postponed by the Florida Supreme Court .	B-PER O O O O O O O O O O O O O B-ORG I-ORG I-ORG O
1784	On Thursday , the 11th Circuit U.S. Court of Appeals in Atlanta denied his appeal in federal court .	O O O O O O B-ORG I-ORG I-ORG I-ORG O B-LOC O O O O O O O

2525	Singapore 's winning campaign to host the World Trade Organisation ( WTO ) 's first ministerial meeting reflected its ambition to play a key role in shaping global free trade , the lifeblood of its economy , analysts said . 2528	The city-state met U.S. opposition two years ago in its bid to host the meeting , expected to gather 4,000 officials from 160 countries from December 9 to 13 .	O O O B-LOC O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O

"	B-PER I-PER I-PER O O O O O B-ORG I-ORG I-ORG I-ORG O B-ORG O O O B-LOC O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O

2834	Woolmer was born in the northern city of Kanpur when his father worked there for an insurance compnay and was himself an active cricketer .	B-PER O O O O O O O B-LOC O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O
